  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_bbd97d3d-9006-41c9-9c73-6b26dec9d5b5'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText13612222955178729237" style="display:none"><i> "Who gives a damn about their reputation? Oh, that would be me! Especially since mine had gone straight to hell in the span of thirty minutes". </i><br /><br />Maysie Ardin is soaking up the summer before her junior year of college, shopping, hanging by the pool and shopping some more. But when her black belt in spending lands her in trouble with her parents, she is forced to take a second job at a local bar to dig herself out of a deep financial pit.<br /><br />She thought she’d be miserable. But then Maysie didn’t count on Jordan Levitt, the hot, pierced and tattooed, drum playing bartender who also happens to be very interested in her. And the feelings are totally mutual.<br /><br />It had the makings of the perfect romantic set up. Boy meets girl. Boy likes girl. Boy has girlfriend? Okay, maybe not.<br /><br />But attraction is a hard thing to ignore and soon Jordan and Maysie find themselves in the middle of a gossip induced firestorm. Maysie has to learn whether she can set aside her fear of public disapproval in order to be with the one she wants. Or will she let the opinions of others dictate her life and her heart?</span>

  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399854ra/774223.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mdn1frJZ3r1rygxh4_zps1418771f.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/sexy%20couples/tumblr_mdn19nClh11rygxh4_zpscfef0c02.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"His voice was like liquid caramel. And I knew exactly what I wanted to do with him. I wanted no holds barred, throw-me-against-a-wall-and-pound-me-within-an-inch-of-my-life-SEX.</b>
</i> <br/>~internal monologue of Maysie<br/><br/><b>And she gets it too. That and then some.</b> **Fans self**<br/><br/>Honestly I don't know where to begin... Here we go!<br/><br/>Maysie Ardin has just been slapped in the face by life when a bill for $3,500.00 comes sending her parents in to</span>
  <span id="freeText15306667030471655872" style="display:none"><b>SPOILER FREE REVIEW</b><br>4 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult/College<br><br><a href="http://s1308.photobucket.com/albums/s607/aim4fashion/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m4xsua0EAk1rx8cbno1_400.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399854i/774222.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/intimate%20gestures/tumblr_mdn1frJZ3r1rygxh4_zps1418771f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399854ra/774223.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mdn1frJZ3r1rygxh4_zps1418771f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/sexy%20couples/tumblr_mdn19nClh11rygxh4_zpscfef0c02.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399854i/774224.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mdn19nClh11rygxh4_zpscfef0c02.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"His voice was like liquid caramel. And I knew exactly what I wanted to do with him. I wanted no holds barred, throw-me-against-a-wall-and-pound-me-within-an-inch-of-my-life-SEX.</b>
</i> <br>~internal monologue of Maysie<br><br><b>And she gets it too. That and then some.</b> **Fans self**<br><br>Honestly I don't know where to begin... Here we go!<br><br>Maysie Ardin has just been slapped in the face by life when a bill for $3,500.00 comes sending her parents in to a tail spin. Now instead of enjoying her summer vacation before her junior year in college spending more money. She must get a second job to pay off her debt.<br><br>When her roommate Riley tells her about a waitress job at a local bar Maysie jumps at the opportunity. They both go and fill out the paper work. And when Maysie looks up and spots Jordan Levitt the bartender she is at a loss for words. Literally.<br><i>The guy is that gorgeous.</i><br><br>The attraction is instant and comes from both sides. They're like magnets drawing to each others raw energy. Jordan makes it abundantly clear he wants Maysie. But things go terribly wrong when she finds out who he is.<br><b>AND who his girlfriend is.</b> <br><br>Maysie continues to fight the undeniable attraction she has for Jordan. Unfortunately no matter how much she puts out the flames.. <b>He keeps lighting the match.</b> <br><br><br><i>
  <b>"But tell me, Mays, why is it all I can think about is you&gt; Why am I so eager to take another guy's head off for touching you? Why is it when I lay in bed at night I dream that it's you there beside me?"</b>
</i> ~Jordan<br><br>So while she is willing to deny deny deny her feelings. He comes at her with the gloves off. <br><br><i>
  <b>'He was flipping Amazing. And I was in so deep that I wasn't sure I could swim to the surface.'</b>
</i> ~Maysie<br><br>She can no longer fight it. So she gives in, not knowing just how bad the consequences will be.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Who gives a damn about their reputation? Oh, that would be me! Especially since mine had gone straight to hell in the span of thirty minutes".</b>
</i> ~Maysie<br><br><b>Rumors spread fast across campus</b><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Random%20quotes%20and%20pics%20with%20words/rumb1_e_1667_ct11rumorsjpg43_zps594bb2c7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399854i/774225.jpg" alt=" photo rumb1_e_1667_ct11rumorsjpg43_zps594bb2c7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Random%20quotes%20and%20pics%20with%20words/gossip2_zps5db211f7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399854i/774226.jpg" alt=" photo gossip2_zps5db211f7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Random%20quotes%20and%20pics%20with%20words/27982463_zps9835a83e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399854i/774227.jpg" alt=" photo 27982463_zps9835a83e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Hearts break and all the rumors lead to a lot of tears...</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/tears%20tears%20and%20more%20tears/tumblr_lg9e9iv02L1qbmi9v.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393027ra/756618.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lg9e9iv02L1qbmi9v.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Unable to deny their need for one another Maysie and Jordan decide to move forward. However jealousy and trust issues plague them brought on from the rocky foundation of their relationship. How can these two survive if everything and everyone seems to be against them. All the drama leads Maysie to ask...<br><b> Is it worth it?</b><br><br><b>Vicious lies.<br><br>Catty females.<br><br>And horny college boys turn Maysie's world upside down. Just because of a kiss. Albeit the kiss was a<i> take your shirt off-let me lick you-pull my dress and give it to me baby in nature.</i><br>Yeah the kiss was that G O O D!!</b><br> <br><br><u>Thoughts</u><br>I loved this book and I totally recommend it.<b> This book puts mean girls in the grave.</b> It will make you mad, real mad but trust me it's worth it.<br>One thing that I really enjoyed was the writing style. Meredith Walters will suck you and never let go. As a matter of fact she still has me, I am a fan for life!LOL!!! The writing is fast paced and solid with plenty of witty banter and steam that will leave you sweaty.<br>The lead characters tug at your heart strings. As they try to do the right thing and fail miserably. And then even as they attempt a relationship you'll want to fight for it yourself. That is how passionate they are. That is how passionate Walters wrote these characters.<br><br><br>Dear readers,<br>I recommend this book to anyone who loves an alpha male with an overprotective streak, steamy panty melting love scenes, intense angst and drama that will last for days and days.<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Love some hate some<br>Writing style- So good it sucks you in to the pages<br>Plot/Storyline- Will have your emotions on chaos levels of high-low<br>Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy -&gt;Panty melting steamy<br>Overall- I loved it!! READ IT! I am officially in PIMP MODE!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then tells us about it on Goodreads!</b><br><br>For more reviews go to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><br><b>
  <i>*ARC provided by author for an honest review*</i>

<div id="review_445932041" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/445932041" />
    <a title="Jenny Levine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12673270-jenny-levine"><img alt="Jenny Levine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353067785p2/12673270.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/445932041?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny Levine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny Levine" href="/user/show/12673270-jenny-levine">Jenny Levine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer445932041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2457092489299152868"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396117ra/763295.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> THIS BOOK PISSED THE LIVING SHIT OUT OF ME!!!! </b><br/><br/>OMG. It took me some time to write a review because Idk where to start because while it annoyed me so much, I actually do love it as well...<br/><br/>Now, am I making any sense? No? <br/>Okay then, I'll just start with my review...<br/>[May contain spoilers]<br/><br/><b> Bad Rep </b> is about sorority girl <b> Maysie </b> who hasn't been doing the best choices lately (Read: 3,500$ credit card bill!!!) Not wanting her parents to save her ass <u> AGAIN </u> and be disappointed at her <u> AGAIN </u>, she dec</span>
  <span id="freeText2457092489299152868" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396117ra/763295.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> THIS BOOK PISSED THE LIVING SHIT OUT OF ME!!!! </b><br><br>OMG. It took me some time to write a review because Idk where to start because while it annoyed me so much, I actually do love it as well...<br><br>Now, am I making any sense? No? <br>Okay then, I'll just start with my review...<br>[May contain spoilers]<br><br><b> Bad Rep </b> is about sorority girl <b> Maysie </b> who hasn't been doing the best choices lately (Read: 3,500$ credit card bill!!!) Not wanting her parents to save her ass <u> AGAIN </u> and be disappointed at her <u> AGAIN </u>, she decided to look for another job (as she has a job in the morning) that she can work for at nights so she can pay her debts. Together with her super awesome friend, <b> Riley, </b> they found a job at a bar called Barton's wherein she meets the guy who's the cause of all the nasty rumors that's going to be spread about her throughout the story, <b> Jordan Levitt. </b><br><br>Tattooed, pierced, rock god <b> Jordan </b> (*cough* NEW BOOK BOYFRIEND *cough*) is instantly attracted to Maysie at their first meeting. There's no denying it on Maysie's part as well. They flirt around and there's a lot of sexual chemistry going on. And soon, they'll find themselves caught up with each other.<br><br>But wait...<br>There's one problem...<br><b> ONE MAJOR PROBLEM... </b><br>...<br>...<br>...<br>...<br>...<br>Our guy Jordan here has a <b> GIRLFRIEND!!! </b><br><br>YUP, you read that right.<br><br>Oh wait, there's more...<br>Maysie freakin' <b> <u> KNOWS his girlfriend. </u> </b><br><br>UH OH.<br><br>Their world came crashing down.<br><br>That's how it all went wrong...<br><br>And, that's when it started to annoy me...<br><br>My reaction while reading:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396117ra/763296.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Notice the lack of status updates? I was sooo infuriated with this book that I didn't put it down because I just want to know what will happen next...okay, that's not true. I am actually afraid because I know there's going to be a lot of struggle and pain, but I'm looking forward for the time they'll get their HEA.<br><br>Oh God. I can't imagine how many times I cursed and bitch slapped everyone from this book in my mind. (Except Riley and Vivian because they're both awesome). Okay, first issue, Jordan:<br> <br>Oh dear Lord. If he's into Maysie so much, why can't he just break up with Olivia?! He said they're not really going strong, but why the hell can't he move on with Maysie. I internally kept screaming on him to: <b> Ditch the bitch!!! </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ He did though. But, it took him a WHOLE LOT OF TIME!!! Like, I got impatient already.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And then, there's Maysie. This girl is a handful. Rumors are spread about her by her sorority sisters, which she doesn't do anything about and can't even stand up for herself, and I hate it that she's so afraid of being removed from their sisterhood. Ugh. Your world doesn't revolve around them sweetie and they're just a bunch of mean plastic bitches so move on, girl. Screw the sisterhood. Gahd.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396117ra/763297.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396117ra/763298.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I'm glad that she DID stand up and defend herself in the end. It was actually the most EPIC scene in the book. Totally loved it!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b> -Rant done- </b><br><br>This review doesn't even cover half the plot of the book. You will meet different types of people here. Relentless bitches who would do everything to get Maysie down. Frat guys who are equally as bitchy as sorority girls. And many more. There are also good people though. <br><br>The thing I really love about this book is Maysie and Jordan's scenes together. Their chemistry is way up high!!! Especially their sexual chemistry, like:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396117ra/763299.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And despite of my frustration and hair pulling attempts while reading, I'm really glad that I didn't take a break from it and read it all the way because the ending was <b> WORTH THE WAIT. </b><br><br><b> <i> “This is for the girl who always runs away,”<br><br>What do I have to do to make you stay?<br>What should I say to make you mine?<br>When will you stop running, girl?<br>I'm watching for the sign.<br><br>You build me up and break me down<br>Over and over again<br>I crave your seductive destruction<br>Even as I long for your pain.<br><br>But it wasn't all bad was it?<br>Things weren't always this way.<br>You filled the space in my empty heart,<br>Your eyes told me things your lips would never say.<br><br>So here I am, watching you run.<br>I wish you'd stop trying to leave.<br>How easy you forget<br>that you're my reason to breathe.<br><br>Stop running, girl<br>It won't always feel like this,<br>Stop running, girl<br>Stop running... </i> </b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <i> “You have taken my<br>heart, every inch of me, Maysie. I don't<br>know that I have anything else to give you<br>that you don't already have.”<br><br>“I love you, Jordan. With everything<br>that I am. And I'm sick of wasting time until<br>we can be together. I don't give a shit about<br>anything or anyone but you and me.” </i>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>OVERALL, <b> I LOVED IT!<br><br>4 STARS! </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_476768825" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/476768825" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/476768825?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=1-2-stars-read">1-2-stars-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer476768825" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6555295782331116386">My Maysie and Jordan:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400744i/777002._SY540_.jpg' width='250' height='320' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400744i/777003._SY540_.jpg' width='250' height='320' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"I wanted to tell you that I couldn't stop thinking about your face. That you had burrowed your way so deep into my veins that I would fucking bleed you. That if I died tomorrow, I could go a happy man for having felt your lips on my skin."</b>
</blockquote><br/>I hate when this happens to me. Interesting story, good writing but NO connection with characters. They were annoying, immature, cheating, mean... Some parts of this book were boring, some were really frustrating, I was really angry wi</span>
  <span id="freeText6555295782331116386" style="display:none">My Maysie and Jordan:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400744i/777002._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400744i/777003._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I wanted to tell you that I couldn't stop thinking about your face. That you had burrowed your way so deep into my veins that I would fucking bleed you. That if I died tomorrow, I could go a happy man for having felt your lips on my skin."</b>
</blockquote><br>I hate when this happens to me. Interesting story, good writing but NO connection with characters. They were annoying, immature, cheating, mean... Some parts of this book were boring, some were really frustrating, I was really angry with character's behaviour and it never captured me. But some parts were enjoyable so I do not regret reading it. Bad Rep was a solid 2.5 stars read for me.<br><br>Jordan was contradictory in his behaviour and there were times when I really did not like him as character. He was so much interested in Maysie from very beginning but he was not able to break up with his longterm girlfriend. He wanted to be together with Maysie, but never really stand up for her when there was a need to do so. In my eyes, he was definitely NOT a kind of hero that readers should look up to. Yes, he was not a bad person and they were times that he made me swoon but overall I just could not love him. And Maysie's temper tautrums? Gross. Annoying. Irritating. Definitely no connection with main characters in this book from my side.<br><br>Fraternity and sorority system was never my thing. In Bad Rep whole Greek system was presented in very bad way and made most of the members look really stupid. So if you are fan of this college system, I would recommend you not to read this book. Fortunatelly, writing style was good and storyline was interesting enough to make me keep reading until the end. <br><br><a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">More reviews on my blog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6555295782331116386" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/470802009?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer470802009" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5887046186719334632"><br/>What if the timing and circumstances were off when you meet your soul mate? <br/><br/>What if he was everything you ever wanted and the attraction was overwhelming?<br/><br/>What if he had a girlfriend for three years and they were considered your college’s ‘it’ couple?<br/><br/>What if his girlfriend was your sorority’s president and your social standing would suffer?<br/><br/>What if he was crazy about you and you acted on it before he closed the door on his prior relationship?<br/><br/>What if your reputation got destroyed?<br/><br/>Would he be worth </span>
  <span id="freeText5887046186719334632" style="display:none"><br>What if the timing and circumstances were off when you meet your soul mate? <br><br>What if he was everything you ever wanted and the attraction was overwhelming?<br><br>What if he had a girlfriend for three years and they were considered your college’s ‘it’ couple?<br><br>What if his girlfriend was your sorority’s president and your social standing would suffer?<br><br>What if he was crazy about you and you acted on it before he closed the door on his prior relationship?<br><br>What if your reputation got destroyed?<br><br>Would he be worth it or would you walk away?<br><br>What if ‘he’ was...Jordan Levitt? <br><br>Could you stay away?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399855i/774229._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Jordan Levitt is a pierced, tatted, bartender, fraternity president and drummer of Generation Rejects. Nickname: Piper – as in Pied Piper of P****- because every girl swoons at his feet. Please note: Jordan sings as well…I know he is AMAZING! He is total alpha and completely head over heels for Maysie.<br><br>This book takes the main character Maysie Ardin (a pleaser type of personality) through some amazing highs and some really crappy lows. She is destroyed socially much like the movie Sorority Wars. <br><br>Maysie endures social hell and lets it get the best of her and at times lets it define her. I have to admit some of her actions were frustrating and maybe I would have handled things differently but I totally understood how she felt. <br> <br>Bad Rep is a very entertaining angsty read, which left my stomach in knots for most of the book. I loved A. Meredith Walters’ writing and Jordan Levitt has landed a spot on my book boyfriend list for sure!!!</span>

<div id="review_559207725" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559207725" />
    <a title="Jenny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/345428-jenny"><img alt="Jenny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592349447p2/345428.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559207725?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny" href="/user/show/345428-jenny">Jenny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559207725" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1733300315709219909">***SPOILERS***<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>I'm honestly at a bit of a loss as to where to start with this screaming hot mess. Maysie is one of the more unlikable characters I've come across in awhile. She's vain. We are repeatedly told how she knows she is hot. She's also an insecure whiney baby and a bit of a jerk. Jordan is whatever the scene calls for him to be with zero consistency. One minute he is a "poet" the next a cheating bad boy then a possessive alpha-male then a charming stand-up guy. All over the place. Honest</span>
  <span id="freeText1733300315709219909" style="display:none">***SPOILERS***<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />I'm honestly at a bit of a loss as to where to start with this screaming hot mess. Maysie is one of the more unlikable characters I've come across in awhile. She's vain. We are repeatedly told how she knows she is hot. She's also an insecure whiney baby and a bit of a jerk. Jordan is whatever the scene calls for him to be with zero consistency. One minute he is a "poet" the next a cheating bad boy then a possessive alpha-male then a charming stand-up guy. All over the place. Honestly, there was zero reason that he wouldn't have just split with Olivia before he hooked up with Maysie if he was half the good guy the author spends the rest of the book trying to convince us he is. There wasn't some big obstacle keeping him with her. I understand sometimes things happen but this was just contrived plotting. The rest of the characters seem to only exists in order to prop up the lives of these two idiots. <br /><br />This book feels like it has multiple personality syndrome. Is this a story about the consequences of hooking up with someone who isn't free? Or about how girls tear each other down? Or about unsupportive parents? Or about not letting your insecurities rule your life? Take your pick because the author takes a swing at all of them but doesn't manage to deliver really on any of them. Instead it just ends up being a mush of blah that goes on and on.<br /><br />Beyond the unlikable characters and uneven storytelling it also needs an editor just to fix things like the author referring to Lemmy from Motörhead as "Lenny" or that the title of the show MythBusters isn't two words. Maysie actually bags on MythBusters at one point...heaven forbid someone around her like something intelligent that doesn't revolve around beer bongs and sorority parties.<br /><br />I'm just grateful that this was a cheap read but, wow, buyer beware...</span>
  <a data-text-id="1733300315709219909" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_471072989" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/471072989" />
    <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag"><img alt="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410910791p2/8191340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/471072989?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=tat-pierced-badboy">tat-pierced-badboy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer471072989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2703865949652241938"><b>New Adult at its best!</b> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774289.gif' width='50' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774289.gif' width='50' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774289.gif' width='50' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774289.gif' width='50' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774290.gif' width='350' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Maisey is an insecure college girl away from her controlling parents with a Father that makes her think she is not good enough. She joins a sorority to help her fit it and feel part of something. She and her roommate Riley, get a job at a local bar, Barton’s for the summer. This is where Maysie meets and falls for bad boy drummer, songwriter, Ducati riding, bartending hottie fully equipped with tats and piercings. His name is Jordan and he happens to be fraternity presiden</span>
  <span id="freeText2703865949652241938" style="display:none"><b>New Adult at its best!</b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774289.gif" width="50" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774289.gif" width="50" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774289.gif" width="50" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774289.gif" width="50" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774290.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maisey is an insecure college girl away from her controlling parents with a Father that makes her think she is not good enough. She joins a sorority to help her fit it and feel part of something. She and her roommate Riley, get a job at a local bar, Barton’s for the summer. This is where Maysie meets and falls for bad boy drummer, songwriter, Ducati riding, bartending hottie fully equipped with tats and piercings. His name is Jordan and he happens to be fraternity president dating the sorioty president. But… Jordan has not loved Olivia for a while now, but has not told her this and she is away for the summer...Uh Oh!<br> <br>There is instant attraction between Mays and Jordan and Jordan wants to get to know Mays a little bit better. Once Maysie finds out Jordan has a girlfriend of three years and this girlfriend is the president of Maysie’s sorority …. Well that kinda puts a screeching halt to pursuing anything with Jordan… <b>or does it?</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399892i/774291.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So begins the roller coaster of events that will test everything Maysie and Jordan feel for one another: Olivia’s return, the parties, the betrayal and lies (Greek sisters can be nasty), the misunderstandings and “the song”… As in most new adult genre angst filled books; there is the drama, drama, drama and this book certainly had it’s share, but it also had a really sweet story of coming into your own and deciding what you want out of life and letting go of what others (including parents) think of you.<br> <br>The author did a very nice job of letting the reader experience what Maysie and Jordan felt and why. I liked how they both dealt with what was happening to them and around them. Yes, there were some bumps in the road and some damn-don’t-do-that moments, but they all played a part in the journey of discovery for this couple. <br><br>I totally loved Riley, Mays’ roommate and even Eli, Mays’ casual “townie” stoner ex-boyfriend had some wise words of advice for Mays; however, my favorite character is Jordan, he just had the whole package from looks, attitude, talent and protectiveness and his sweet loving sexy moves were *Rawr*<br> <br>Jordan Levitt makes it to my book boyfriend list. <span>[image error]</span><br><br>I borrowed this image from the authors facebook page:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399892i/774292.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><b>“Stop over thinking it, Mays. Don’t think about Olivia, or your sisters, or anybody else. I want you to only think about me. And us. And what my fingers are doing right now. The rest we can figure out later…together"</b><br><br><b>“I’ve never gone raw before, baby. I’m afraid it’ll be over before we even start if I go much quicker.”</b><br><br><b>“Jordan, it’s okay. You may be called the pied piper of pussy. But the only pussy you’ll be touching is mine.”</b><br><br><b>“I thought you were worth everything. That we were worth all the drama and bullshit. I am willing to fight to the death for what we have. But I can only do that if you’re willing to fight with me.”</b><br><br><u>And… you will have to read this book to find out if Maisey could handle the “Bad Rep” and allow herself the love and devotion of Jordan Levitt.</u><br><br><br><b>"But it was the drummer who maintained the heartbeat of the music. It was impossible to look anywhere but at him"</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399892i/774293.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Here is a verse from the song Jordan wrote for Maisey</i><br><br><b>"This is for the girl who always runs away"</b><br><br><br><b>What do I have to do to make you stay?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774294.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>What should I say to make you mine?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399892ra/774295.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>When will you stop running girl?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399893ra/774296.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><br><b>I'm watching for the sign</b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399893ra/774297.gif" width="150" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://amzn.to/T9WTBQ" rel="nofollow noopener">It's Out Now! Get it here</a><br><br>*Thank-you so much to the author for providing an ARC for review. Release date is scheduled for <b>12-21-12</b> So... mark your calendar!</span>

<div id="review_448749325" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/448749325" />
    <a title="Kim Person" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7590856-kim-person"><img alt="Kim Person" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434694589p2/7590856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/448749325?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim Person" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim Person" href="/user/show/7590856-kim-person">Kim Person</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7590856-kim-person?shelf=rock-roll">rock-roll</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7590856-kim-person?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer448749325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15211150965225995477">First I must thank A. Meredith Walters for allowing me to read an advanced copy of Bad Rep! Anyone, that knows me knows I have serious obssession with Rock Stars so as always when I got the book I just.....<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380379126ra/735227.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is seriously a wonderful read. The book is told from Maysie's POV and I think it had to be in order to understand that how much at one time other's opinions mattered more to her than what she thought of herself. Maysie is a Junior in College and part of a sorority. Well, due to her hog wi</span>
  <span id="freeText15211150965225995477" style="display:none">First I must thank A. Meredith Walters for allowing me to read an advanced copy of Bad Rep! Anyone, that knows me knows I have serious obssession with Rock Stars so as always when I got the book I just.....<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380379126ra/735227.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is seriously a wonderful read. The book is told from Maysie's POV and I think it had to be in order to understand that how much at one time other's opinions mattered more to her than what she thought of herself. Maysie is a Junior in College and part of a sorority. Well, due to her hog wild spending spree on the credit card her parent's gave her for emergency's she receives a lovely letter from the rents telling her she will be paying them back. Okay, so what's girl who is taking summer courses, has one job already, and a full social calendar to do? That's right go with your BFF and roommate, Riley, and get a second job.<br><br>So off to Barton's Bar &amp; Grille the girl's go and what's waiting for her when she is handed her application is the the MOST gorgeous boy she's ever seen. Freaking hot as hell, tattooed, piereced, frat boy that is a drummer in a hot local band,Generation Sin, stands Jordan and for the first time ever Maysie, the girl who always has a boyfriend but was able to remain detached, is speechless. Maysies eyes meet Jordan's and she ...........<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764405.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well maybe not that bad but damn I would be! Jordan just happens to be a 21 year-old bartender at Barton's. And boy oh boy can does he flirt with Maysie..............<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764406.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to take a moment and talk about Riley. She is freaking hysterical with her witty and dry humor and awesome come backs. She takes no sh*t and she tells you like it is. Aren't those the best friends to have? Well the girls both get waitressing jobs at Barton's that same day and come back later that night to "shadow" the more experienced wait staff. I laughed my head off when Riley met Cal and Tito the two line cooks. I was seriously.........<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/428029.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay so back to my fav's Jordan &amp; Maysie. They have instant connection you can feel the sparks flying when they are in the same room or as Riley so aptly put it "Good God, the sexual tension is giving me hives." But hey wouldn't you be thinking sexual thoughs, positions, naked thoughts if this was staring at you..........<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396549i/764407.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I sure the hell would be. So Jordan asks Maysie to hang out with him after work so they can get to know one other better and Maysie is all for that until three of her sorority sisters come into Barton's and she learns that Jordan is TAKEN very TAKEN by Olivia the President of Maysie's sorority. Jordan forgot to share that tidbit yep he's been dating Olivia for three years and he just happens to be the President of his fraternity. So yeah this is the part where I went.........<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764408.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why the hell did he ask her out if he was taken? Well, he tries to explain that the relationship is "strained" but Maysie puts it to him in black &amp; white - NO WAY - she's not going to do that to her sweet sorority sister who according to Maysie just hapens to be beyond beautiful, perfect, popular- get the picture? Maysie with all her self-doubt starts to quesion what would a guy like Jordan see in her anyway.<br><br>So all summer long the two of them dance around each other. Constant eye contact......<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/581390.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maysie continues her pseudo relationship with "townie" Eli whe she describes as the stoner who plays guitar and with one kiss could make her forget everything BUT that was before Jordan..after Jordan enter's the picture it's bye bye Eli....The book starts to pick up speed pretty quickly you feel the tension between Maysie &amp; Jordan and something just has to give. Maysie comes in to Barton's on one of her nights off to get her drink on and Eli also comes in. He is ALL over her and Jordan is seeing red. He is seriously............<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386302ra/745725.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Jordan finally initiates the first......<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393466ra/757556.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Olivia returns the real agnst starts to set in and I swear Olivia's so called BFF, Milla, is the biggest b**tch! I hated her in this book! Things went from .............<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764409.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>to well this.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764410.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and then everything goes to hell in a handbasket as you might suspect. There were parts of this book where I was.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764411.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>and I was definitely...........<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764412.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bad Rep ultimately has a message,HUGE ONE, and when you read it you will see. This is an amazing book! I freaking adored it! I'm utterly in love with it. Jordan and his tongue ring well I'm sure you can imagine. I was so.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764413.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I feel in love with everything about Jordan &amp; Maysie. They are MEANT to be together! When I was done with this book I was...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396549ra/764414.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes my family is used to me and my insanely happy moments.<br><br>Well when all was said and done I got myself the angst, the sexy as sin Rock God tattooed &amp; pierced drummer Jordan, off the charts hot between the sheets, biggest damn smile on my face right now and fantastic lesson learned about being yourself and not caring what others think/say!!!<br><br>Another 5++++++ read! Hot damn there are some awesome books coming out in December!!!! If this isn't on your TBR well damn add it! This is one seriously rocking book! I can't wait for it's release so EVERYONE can experience what I did while reading Bad Rep. FREAKING ADORE THIS BOOK!! I absolutely adore A.Meredith Walters :)<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16102880.Bad_Rep" title="Bad Rep by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1351282857s/16102880.jpg" alt="Bad Rep by A. Meredith Walters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_471238472" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/471238472" />
    <a title="Airah ♔" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12508358-airah"><img alt="Airah ♔" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383964726p2/12508358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/471238472?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Airah ♔" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Airah ♔" href="/user/show/12508358-airah">Airah ♔</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=genre_contemporary">genre_contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=swoon-worthy-heroes">swoon-worthy-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=what-a-badass">what-a-badass</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=rockstars-and-celebrities">rockstars-and-celebrities</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=2013-favorites">2013-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12508358-airah?shelf=just-freaking-awesome">just-freaking-awesome</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer471238472" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11601221926428138984"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"One day, I’ll get you a ring on your finger. You just wait and see."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399918ra/774369.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Aww. Seriously. One of the best New Adult novels I’ve read recently!</b><br/><br/>With all the sorority drama going on in this book, <b>Bad Rep</b> clearly has more issues than the movie <b>Mean Girls</b>.<br/><br/>Everything started with the $3500 credit card statement from a weekend trip to Virginia Beach:<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>My Visa was supposed to be used “in emergencies only.” My parents had given me a 5,000 dollar limit, stressing that I was NEVER to even think abo</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11601221926428138984" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"One day, I’ll get you a ring on your finger. You just wait and see."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399918ra/774369.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Aww. Seriously. One of the best New Adult novels I’ve read recently!</b><br><br>With all the sorority drama going on in this book, <b>Bad Rep</b> clearly has more issues than the movie <b>Mean Girls</b>.<br><br>Everything started with the $3500 credit card statement from a weekend trip to Virginia Beach:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>My Visa was supposed to be used “in emergencies only.” My parents had given me a 5,000 dollar limit, stressing that I was NEVER to even think about using it. Unless I was broken down on the other side of a deserted highway with a serial killer hot on my tail.</b>
</blockquote><br>In case you’re wondering, that would be <b>Maysie Ardin</b>, our female MC. She’s a people pleaser. Loves the sorority so much and can’t drop it like a bad habit even when things went downhill. Because of her immense credit, she needed another part-time job… fast.<br><br>Ended up waitressing at Barton's.<br><br>Meet <b>Jordan Levitt</b> – Does bartending job at Barton’s. He’s a drummer from the Generation Rejects band. A pussy magnet according to bandmates. President of the Pi Sig house. Said to be the most popular guy at Rinard College.<br><br><i>And before I forgot</i>, because Jordan himself forgot to tell our female MC here while he’s chasing her… he’s the boyfriend of Maysie’s sorority president, Olivia.<br><br><b>Now, things just got a little more interesting.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399918ra/774370.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, I know nothing about the Greek system aside from the stuff I watched on TV. But the sorority/fraternity events going on here seemed pretty realistic and enjoyable.<br><br>This book was really well-written. And the best thing about this book is the consistent character development. <br><br>Other people might get really annoyed at how insecure Maysie could be… but then who wouldn’t be insecure when your boyfriend’s ex-gf is as gorgeous and as popular as Olivia Peer <b>and</b> the relationship you have was built on lies?<br><br>Anyway, I just loved how Maysie matured throughout the book! Thank God for her bestfriend and recently roomie, <b>Riley</b>. She supported Maysie through the good and the bad times!<br><br>My favorite part of the bad times? Why, she just slapped and yanked her hair. I know that was totally uncalled for but I’m pretty wistful here. Indeed, tough love coming from bestfriends can put someone out of one’s funk.<br><br>The other secondary characters in this book were amazing too!<br><br><b>Vivian</b> and <b>Gracie</b>. Wow! They’re the ultimate sidekicks. They’re the best sorority sisters out there!<br><br>I even liked <b>Eli</b>, Maysie’s townie ex-hookup. I thought he was this great douchebag but then he redeemed himself by giving Maysie the most helpful advice throughout the book:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Well, shit, Mays. Then you need to fight for him. Don’t give up on something like that. It doesn’t come along very often. And when you find it, you hold on tight. You lock that shit down with an iron fist and you never, ever let go. Even when life tries to take it from you, you smack life upside its head like a little bitch and you keep on fighting for it. You hear me?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh btw, be sure to be on the lookout for the <b>lunchroom scene</b>. It’s my favorite part of the book. I actually re-read it a couple of times. Maysie finally put on her big girl panties! Way to go girl!!<br><br>I would like to end this review with the song Jordan wrote for Maysie, just so I would always remember why I fell in love with this book in the first place. I have this thing for songs written for the female lead. I feel giddy everytime. It’s like they’re written for me. HAHA<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>What do I have to do to make you stay?<br>What should I say to make you mine?<br>When will you stop running, girl?<br>I’m watching for the sign.<br><br>You build me up and break me down<br>Over and over again<br>I crave your seductive destruction<br>Even as I long for your pain<br><br>But it wasn’t all bad was it?<br>Things weren’t always this way.<br>You filled the space in my empty heart,<br>Your eyes told me things your lips would never say.<br><br>So here I am, watching you run.<br>I wish you’d stop trying to leave.<br>How easy you forget<br>That you’re my reason to breathe.<br><br>Stop running, girl.<br>I’ve got nowhere to go.<br>I’ll wait until forever <br>I promise to take this slow.<br><br>Stop running, girl.<br>It won’t always feel like this.<br>Stop running, girl.<br>Stop running, girl!</b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="11601221926428138984" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478733449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16399207959380700362"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099887._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099888._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So let's start with the most important part. I, Smitten, am totally in <i>love</i> with Jordan Levitt! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099889._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>5 stars for Jordan and Maysie!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099890.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385218694i/7100529._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Awwww, this book is so good. Firstly, you have to know, I have a hell of a lot going on in my life at the moment, so finding a book that can hold my attention is difficult. I'm only getting short periods of time to read and I'm finding things just aren't holding my interest so well... and then I picked up <i>Bad Rep</i>.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099891.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well, the first day I started it, I was terribly late for w</span>
  <span id="freeText16399207959380700362" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099887._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099888._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So let's start with the most important part. I, Smitten, am totally in <i>love</i> with Jordan Levitt! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099889._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>5 stars for Jordan and Maysie!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099890.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385218694i/7100529._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Awwww, this book is so good. Firstly, you have to know, I have a hell of a lot going on in my life at the moment, so finding a book that can hold my attention is difficult. I'm only getting short periods of time to read and I'm finding things just aren't holding my interest so well... and then I picked up <i>Bad Rep</i>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099891.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, the first day I started it, I was terribly late for work. A. Meredith Walters, I hold you solely responsible for that. It still took me a week to get through, due to 'real life' crap, but it was so nice to know that I had a book that would whisk me off into a dream world and allow me to forget every day life, at the end of a long day.<br><br>That, for me, is what reading is about. Escapism, losing yourself in a story and immersing yourself in the words on the page and the lives of these fictional characters. <i>Bad Rep</i> offered exactly that.<br><br>This is the story of Maysie Ardin and Jordan Levitt. They meet when Maysie takes on a job at a local bar, where Jordan works, to pay off her debts. The insta-lust is unavoidable and the connection between these two characters is palpable.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099892._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Every love song I write now is because of you. Every song I will ever write for the rest of my life will be because of you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>However, despite the instant undeniable attraction between tattooed, bad boy, drummer/barman, Jordan and sassy sorority girl, Maysie, it isn't all plain sailing. Jordan has a girlfriend. And not just any girlfriend... his girlfriend is president of Maysie's sorority and he has been with her for three long years.<br>So both Jordan and Maysie do everything they can to ignore the pull that they feel between them every time they are in the same room. But how long can they pretend they feel nothing for one another? And when things get heated, how will they fair under the scrutiny and judgement of others?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099893._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I thought you were worth everything. That we were worth all the drama and bullshit. I am willing to fight to the death for what we have. But I can only do that if you're willing to fight with me.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Now, some people are going to want to black list this book immediately. It <i>does</i> include cheating. However... I have learnt a lot about what I find acceptable and unacceptable when reading. I have to just stress, my views regarding fictional characters do <i>not</i> match my views regarding real life, but hey, that's the beauty of reading, right? It's not real and we can be a lot more liberal and naughty than we would get away with in the real world. ;)<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I don't like seeing some other guy touching you. Not when it should be me touching you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>So, it turns out, I can accept pretty much anything as long as it is in the name of love. If the motive of the character is that they have done something, perhaps something terrible, because they love the other character... I can deal. However, if they betray trust or break my heart for no good reason or simply because they made an error in judgement, I'm a lot less forgiving.<br><br>I've also learnt that I can accept cheating if it is between the two main characters. If one of my main characters cheats on the other, I'm done. I cant cope with that and I can't forgive it. However, if the two characters I love cheat <i>with</i> one another, I can totally get over it. I know, I know. I have disgusting double standards and I should be completely ashamed... but meh, suck it up, that's the way it is. :p<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099894._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>His voice was like liquid caramel. And I knew exactly what I wanted to do with him. I wanted no holds barred, throw-me-against-a-wall-and-pound-me-within-an-inch-of-my-life-SEX. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099895._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, now we've delved into the inner workings of Smitten's conscience, lets talk about <i>Bad Rep</i> some more.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Who gives a damn about their reputation? Oh, that would be me.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I really liked Maysie. She's real. Yes she spends too much money on designer clothing, yes she's insecure, yes she really can be a bit of a bitch and yes she over reacts to some things. But if you tell me you aren't guilty one or all of those things, I'll tell you to get your head out of your ass! Hey, we're women, it's our prerogative to go from an insecure mess to uber-bitch-from-hell in 0.2 seconds flat, right?!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Hey, Mays," Jordan yelled from behind me. I grudgingly turned back around, my back straight and my face blank.<br>"Yeah?"<br>Jordan cocked his head to the side, his eyes burning into mine. "Jaz may be pretty, but you're fucking gorgeous," he called out loud enough for me to hear over the thumping base of the band. He grinned at me and the freaking winked. I hated and loved it when he did that.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And then there's Jordan. Ohhhh my goodness! He could not be more perfect. I know it's wrong but I just lapped up the fact that he just <i>had</i> to have Maysie. He was head over heels from the very beginning and it was super hot! He's got piercings, tattoos and he plays the freakin' drums!!! Two words... Drummers. Arms. ❤ <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099896.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was sold already, and then he went and did all these naughty, forbidden things to Maysie with his fingers and his tongue, when he really shouldn't be doing them... Ohhh my... Stick a fork in me, I was D.O.N.E! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He was gorgeous, he played in a band, he was a freaking frat boy and he had the whole tattoo, piercing thing going on. I was very aware of what he was, without knowing any more than that.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099897.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Urgh, the angst in this book. It's scrummy! Maysie really battles with what she knows is right and wrong, what she wants and what she feels she should do, how she feels and what everybody else thinks... it's a constant internal war for Maysie and I really wanted to simultaneously hold her hand through it and kick her up the ass!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You have taken my heart, every inch of me Maysie. I don't know that I have anything else to give you that you don't already have." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I <i>hate</i> bullying with a vengeance and have been known for being a little feisty, so I really wanted to maim Olivia and Milla at so many points in the book. Honestly, I <i>hated</i> them so much. Ok, I get that Olivia was hurting and that she was wronged, but seriously, there is a limit and she crossed it... over and over! Bitch needed taking down a peg or two. Her and her little ho of a sidekick.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099898._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I hated how Maysie took the majority of the rap for her and Jordan's actions and he got away pretty lightly. I mean, I know his frat brothers were assholes too, but Maysie went through absolute hell and Jordan kinda seemed to get off easy.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099899.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However, I loved the surrounding characters that had Maysie's back. Riley, Gracie and Vivian are all great and really provide that feeling of camaraderie and sisterhood, ironically, despite the lack of sisterhood shown with Maysie's sorority. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Stop it!" she hissed. I frowned and rubbed my arm. "What are you talking about?" I whispered back. Riley pointed at me, waggling her finger. "I know that look on your face! You're picturing him naked with you naked.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Ok, I think I've mumbled on enough now. And you can probably get that I really loved this book. I've enjoyed A. Meredith Walter's writing before, so I did expect to enjoy <i>Bad Rep</i> and it didn't disappoint! Get involved.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099900._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Bad Rep</i> Statistics</b><br><b>• Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥<br><b>• Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>• Length:</b> 374 pages<br><b>• Narrative:</b> Maisey's POV. First person. Past tense.<br><b>• Series:</b> ✓ <br><b>• Reading Order:</b> <br>- Book #1 - Bad Rep (Bad Rep, #1) <br>- Book #2 - Perfect Regret (Bad Rep, #2) <br><b>• Can this be read as a standalone?</b> Yes<br><b>• Themes:</b><br>Love triangle<br>Rock star romance<br>College romance<br><b>• WARNING. This book includes...</b> <br>Sexual content. Cheating<br><b>• Writing:</b> Great<br><br><a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Bad-Rep-Meredith-Walters-ebook/dp/B00AQQDG1I/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1385214074&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=bad+rep+meredith+walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756313._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
