  <span id="freeText14645674755557183452" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/awesome2_zps7aca9b17.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400140i/775049.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Sweet little baby Jesus <br>I LOVED THIS!</b><br><br><i>**I do need to say that although this book is essentially about cheating. I kinda condoned it. In real life cheating is not cool! Fiction sometimes it is.. like with this.. and Kellan Kyle**</i><br><br><u>
  <b>THE STORY</b>
</u> <br><br>Maysie Arden has always wanted to be popular. <br>Wants everyone to like her. <br>As she has always striven for her parents approval but has never got it. <br><br>When she moves away to College that happens. <br>She gets a hippie/vegan straight shooter best friend Riley.<br>Joins the Chi Delta Sorority <br>And scores her self a “townie” boyfriend. <br><br>Unfortunately after hanging with her “sisters” she has blown her credit card up! <br>Her parents refuse to pay for it so she goes and gets another job.<br><br>While applying for the position at Barton’s she meets the very edible bartender. .<br>He is the very HAAWWTT, tattooed and pierced, drumming/singing extraordinaire Jordan Levitt. <br><b>
  <i>He was this weird mixture of tatted up bad boy and gorgeous boy next door. – Maysie inner monologue. </i>
</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/jordan_zpsbf7db443.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400140i/775050._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Just imagine an eyebrow piercing ok?<br><br>The chemistry between them is INSTANT! <br><br><b>
  <i> Dear lord, the flash of his gleaming white teeth was like a hot button to my nether regions. Down vagina! Down, girl. </i>
</b> Maysie inner monologue<br><br>She couldn’t be happier when he asks her out. <br>Until her “sisters” come into the bar and she finds out who he is… <br><br>And who his girlfriend is…<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m1vnbtDWMl1r37xnm.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397578ra/767243.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And that she knows her…<br>No wonder he looked familiar <br><br>And one half of the golden couple of the school . <br>His girlfriend is Olivia, her Sorority’s President. He’s the president of the Fraternity, <br><br><br>He tried to explain that he would of told her about Olivia but he feels drawn to Maysie, he can’t explain but he wants to get to know her. <br><br>Maysie denies him.<br><br>As much as she wants him she can’t do that to Olivia. <br><br>It just gets so hard. He is so perfect for her… and he won’t stop pursuing her… <br><br>They are like moth’s to the flame..<br><br>Drawn to each other… <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/sexualfrustration-1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398428ra/770002.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But he is still with Olivia… <br><br><b>
  <i>”Why would it matter to you what he was doing? You and I have nothing, are nothing. More to the point there is no such thing as you and I!” I hissed. “You have a girlfriend, Jordan.” <br>	“It matters to me Mays. It matters a lot. I don’t like seeing some other guy touching you. Not when it should be me touching you. I hated him calling you “his girl”. Because I want you all to myself,” he dropped his voice into a seductive growl. <br><br>“I’ve never felt this way about anyone. Ever,” he told me. <br> “Not even with Olivia?” I cringed internally, hating myself for bringing her name into this. But I needed to. It had to be dealt with. Jordan needed to be reminded her had a girlfriend. <br>“Yes. Even with Olivia. Maysie I have a girlfriend. A girlfriend I’ve been with for three goddamn years. But tell me, Mays, why is it that all I can fucking think about is you? Why am I so eager to take another guys head off for touching you? Why is it when I lay in bed at night I wish it was you there beside me?” </i>
</b> **SIGH**<br><br><br>Eventually they give into each other…<br><br>It just happens to be a Frat Party at Jordan’s house. With his GF there. <br><br>They are BUSTED by his GF’s BFF and VP of the Chi Delta’s. <br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m6ywmrPrZI1rncp8a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/403241.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And the shit hits the fan! <br><br>A cat fight is had between Olivia and Maysie and end with Jordan taking Olivia inside.. <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/backstab-women-knife_zps677a630f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400140i/775051.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maysie is boycotted by her sisters, evil rumors are spread throughout the school… <br>Not just from the one night they gave in.. <br>About Maysie… horrible things are said <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/thosebitches_zpsa4b38fbc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400140ra/775052.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She thinks Jordan chose Olivia as he left with her… … <br><br>Turns out that Jordan hasn’t left her alone! He wants her. Be damned what others say! <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/hatersgunnahate.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400140ra/775053.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>”I wanted to tell you that I couldn’t stop thinking about your face. That you have burrowed your way so deep into my veins that I would fucking bleed you. That if I died tomorrow, I could go a happy man for having felt your lips on my skin.”</i>
</b> – Jordan <br><br>But Maysie just can’t help but care about her reputation. <br>Jordan doesn’t care. <br>But she can’t help but let them get to her. <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/99_zps86f54cbf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400140i/775054.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>I just wish I could stop feeling like Kelly Taylor splitting up Dylan and Brenda. Oh crap. I was totally Kelly! I hated Kelly! My own feelings of shame and guilt were burning a hole through my heart. </i>
</b> --Inner thought Maysie<br><br><br>Throw in an Alpha Male, a lot of insecurities, BITCHES, assholes and the rumor mill <br><br>Can they survive it? <br><br>Can something beautiful come from something that started so ugly? <br><br><b>
  <u>MY THOUGHTS</u>
</b> <br><br>I really like this book. I was hooked from the first page. <br><br>Jordan has officially become one of my book boyfriends.. Seriously up there with Travis, Kellan, Hunter, Andrew, Chase and Jace. <i>(In case you haven’t heard of these names. 1 WHERE HAVE U BEEN?!?! And 2 they are from Beautiful Disaster, Thoughtless, Liberating Lacey, The Edge of Never, Chasing Eight and The Mortal Instruments.)</i> <br><br>He is a drummer.. but he sings and WRITES SONGS! Ugh the song! Just beautiful <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/iloveyou.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395954ra/762911.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maysie however… at time’s I just wanted too.. too…<br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/youredead.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400140ra/775055.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Some of the shit she said and did… AGGHH <br>Who gives a shit about your rep if you have JORDAN LEVITT?!?! <br><br>When she hurt Jordan&gt; I WANTED TO CRAWL INTO THE BOOK AND HURT HER! STUPID BITCH! <br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/whatthehelliswrongwithu_zps2f4bee5c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400140ra/775056.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ok but it needed to be said or we wouldn’t have the awesome book we did would we? <br><br>The secondary characters were good.. There weren’t THAT many but enough to get to know who was the good guy who was the bad guy. <br><br>Jordan’s band members were a good laugh…. And serious when they needed to be adding a nice touch. <br><br>The sorority girls?! UGH BITCHES! <br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/bitchplease_zps14b4cafe.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400140i/775057._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Being Aussie we don’t have sororities here.. so all I know of them are what I read or see in Movies… and in the movies the President is always a snotty UP HER SELF BEAUTIFUL BITCH… is that always the way?! <i>Just out of curiosity</i> OK back to the book! <br>Olivia didn’t start out that way <br><br>Riley was good fun- knowing how to handle Maysie when she went off into her depression and also make her laugh <br><br>Maysie’s parents?! What HORRIBLE PEOPLE! UGH <br><br>Sex Scenes?! <b>OFF THE CHARTS HAAWWWTTT</b><br><br><a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/turnedon_zpsf3ede9ae.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398403ra/769906.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Let’s just say that Jordan def knew what he was doing! GAH the man is a GOD in my eyes! <br><br><br>There was a showdown when Maysie couldn’t take any more of the shit…<i>(thank god I got tired of screaming!</i> <a href="http://s1150.beta.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/speakupbitch_zpsde403a73.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400140ra/775058.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> and damn it made me smile!<br><br><br>So all in all… <br><br>Is you like rocky romance, cocky-HAWT-melt your panties with one stare or smirk- tattooed-pierced-bad boy/good guys, angst, an annoying heroine that you learn to like and lots and lots of sex.. Then this is for you! <br></span>

<div id="review_471387356" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/471387356" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/471387356?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer471387356" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17129517932481279981"><b>
  <i>“No more running.” “I’m all run out, baby. You caught me fair and square.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Maysie is a college student who has to get a second summer job to pay her parents back some money she owes them for overspending on her ‘emergency only’ credit card- I mean new shoes are sort of an emergency, right? She and her best friend, Riley decide to apply at a restaurant/bar called Barton’s. They both get hired on right away and meet the bartender Jordan. <b> Holy bad boy Batman! </b>I fell in love with this story (and</span>
  <span id="freeText17129517932481279981" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“No more running.” “I’m all run out, baby. You caught me fair and square.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Maysie is a college student who has to get a second summer job to pay her parents back some money she owes them for overspending on her ‘emergency only’ credit card- I mean new shoes are sort of an emergency, right? She and her best friend, Riley decide to apply at a restaurant/bar called Barton’s. They both get hired on right away and meet the bartender Jordan. <b> Holy bad boy Batman! </b>I fell in love with this story (and Jordan...) How much did I love Jordan? Perfect book boyfriend...<br /><br /><b>
  <i>He was gorgeous, he played in a band, he was a freaking frat boy and he had the whole tattoo, piercing thing going on. </i>
</b><br /><br /> He and Maysie have this whole instant attraction thing going on and they really hit it off. Sounds perfect, right? Maysie thinks so too, until she finds out.... Jordan has a girlfriend. Not just any girlfriend, but president of Maysie’s sorority, all around perfect Olivia. <br /><br />Maysie was a relatable character, she aggravated me at times, but I really liked her. I was proud of her. She had an instant connection with Jordan and tons of chemistry, and she stayed away for the longest time because he had a girlfriend. But she can’t stay away forever... Not with Jordan chasing her the way he did. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“I wanted to tell you that I couldn’t stop thinking about your face. That you had burrowed your way so deep into my veins that I would fucking bleed you. That if I died tomorrow, I could go a happy man for having felt your lips on my skin.”</b>
</i><br /><br />They both made some poor decisions, and unfortunately, Maysie got caught in all the drama, backstabbing, cat-fights, and jealousy of her sorority sisters. Some of them were pretty terrible to her. I felt for Maysie, especially because she is the type of person who cares what other people think. I’m glad she had some good friends (Riley, Grace and Vivian) on her side. <br /><br />Jordan was just ridiculously hot. He was a bad boy/good guy, musician, had tattoo’s and piercings, was a protective alpha male and he stood up for Maysie- especially with her father and some of the sorority/fraternity douche bags. Oh and he was totally swoon worthy! <br /><br /><b><i>“Every song I write now is because of you. Every song I will ever write for the rest of my life will be because of you.”<br /><br />“Your right, baby. We began out of something ugly. But what we became was something beautiful. I just wish I could make you see that.”<br /><br />“You have taken my heart, every inch of me, Maysie. I don’t know that I have anything else to give you that you don’t already have.”</i>  </b><br /><br />The book was angsty, steamy and funny! The ending made me so happy <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Not only did they end up together, but Maysie started sticking up for herself! You go girl!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Maysie’s rant was one of the best parts of the book... <i>”And I don’t give a fuck if you like me. Or if the Chi Delt’s think I’m the biggest whore this side of the Appalachian Mountatins. I am done worrying about what everyone thnks about me. Because all that counts is that I like me. So the rest of you can go to hell.</i> That is an awesome message! Loved the book, loved the characters! </span>
  <a data-text-id="17129517932481279981" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_494561864" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/494561864" />
    <a title="Samantha Rue" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8359659-samantha-rue"><img alt="Samantha Rue" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347346263p2/8359659.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/494561864?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha Rue" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha Rue" href="/user/show/8359659-samantha-rue">Samantha Rue</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8359659-samantha-rue?shelf=couldn-t-finish">couldn-t-finish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8359659-samantha-rue?shelf=mary-sue">mary-sue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8359659-samantha-rue?shelf=twific-bingo">twific-bingo</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer494561864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14313043397573033985">I somehow made it to chapter 5 of this thing, which is kind of miraculous since I spent most of it rolling my eyes, complaining, and laughing (at you, not with you).<br/><br/>Most of the problem was that it's just not my cuppa tea, but there's no denying that the characters are just... not good. <br/><br/>The main character is a blatant Mary Sue. The love interest, Jordan, is 'perfect', and a bad boy (because he's got like piercings and tattoos and stuff! Sooo bad!) even though he's actually a frat boy, and every g</span>
  <span id="freeText14313043397573033985" style="display:none">I somehow made it to chapter 5 of this thing, which is kind of miraculous since I spent most of it rolling my eyes, complaining, and laughing (at you, not with you).<br /><br />Most of the problem was that it's just not my cuppa tea, but there's no denying that the characters are just... not good. <br /><br />The main character is a blatant Mary Sue. The love interest, Jordan, is 'perfect', and a bad boy (because he's got like piercings and tattoos and stuff! Sooo bad!) even though he's actually a frat boy, and every girl totally creams their panties over him. He's described by a coworker as 'unattainable'. <br /><br />Main character describes herself (while looking at herself in the mirror, and no protagonist has ever done that, am I right?) as pretty attractive.<br /><br />The main character is also wildly shallow, it's almost impossible to relate to her. There's tons of internal dialog (did I mention this is in first person?) about how badly she wants to bone these two guys, and almost as if ~against her will~, her body will respond to their voices and actions, which will inevitably lead to such deep introspective narrative as:<br /><br />"What was wrong with me?   I had just got hopelessly turned on by the guy I was sort of seeing and now I'm getting even more turned on thinking about my new co-worker!   My hormones were seriously out of whack!"<br /><br />...and... <br /><br />"Dear lord, the flash of his gleaming white teeth was like a hot button to my nether regions.   Down vagina!   Down, girl."<br /><br />She describes herself as a 'bitch in heat'. She blushes constantly. First time meeting Jordan the Not-Really Bad Boy, she's at a loss for words, so stunned is she by his Bad Boy Beauty (we're just told this is a fact, and never really shown exactly why he's so hot, unless waxing about those piercings and tattoos count [spoiler alert: it doesn't]).<br /><br />When another girl tries to mack on her 'man' (which isn't even Jordan the Not-Really Bad Boy), the main character refers to her as 'bimbo Barbie' and 'crabbed out ho'. She's kind of ridiculously possessive of her boyfriend given that she describes him as sloppy and unmotivated, just some grungy stoner dude with no desire to attend college, which is something that makes her physical attraction to him 'disgust' her.<br /><br />Jordan's eyes smolder, what a panty-dropper~! <br /><br />Plus, he's in college! <br /><br />Score!<br /><br />Despite him being so unattainable and, like omg the hottest guy ever! He's instantly all over the main character, winking and rubbing against her and asking her out, flirting up a storm. Right off the bat. They know nothing about each other. By chapter 4, she's 100% self-aware that what she feels for Jordan is more than simple lust and attraction, but instead a ~TRUE CONNECTION~, even though they've only had a whopping 2 interactions at that point.<br /><br />Her first night waitressing at the restaurant that Jordan also bartends for (the first day they meet, mind), and at what the character describes as a moment in the night so busy that "They had a crowd three people deep all the way around the bar", her and Jordan take a pause in working to dance and grind against each other right in the middle of the crowd of patrons. <br /><br />Like, what? What employee does that on their first day? Or ever? Without getting fired? I know, it's fiction. But damn. They're just so unlikable. <br /><br />Oh yeah, and she got this job without even having to give an interview. And she shirks work to bump-and-grind in front of the customers. Where do I apply?<br /><br />The only saving grace here is the main character's friend and roommate Riley. She's obviously meant to be the voice of reason, but often comes off as annoyingly judgmental. I mean, I can't blame her, this girl needs guidance, but at times she just got on my nerves. <br /><br />I made it right up until Jordan the Not-Really Bad Boy got up on stage to play with his band. He plays drums, writes lyrics, and also sings, even though he's not the lead singer. I'm pretty sure he'd be playing lead guitar if the author could swing it. Maybe being in a band is what makes him a Bad Boy? The piercings and tattoos are mentioned again. HE IS BAD OKAY.<br /><br />But then he sings to the Main Character (IT'S ONLY CHAPTER FIVE), complete with ~lyrics~ and crooning screams of, "Fuck Me!" into the microphone, and it's just so cheesy and squicky and ridiculous that I had to erase this thing from my kindle because even the thought of the memory of it embarrasses me. <br /><br />The formatting was good and I only spotted one error. For what it's worth...?</span>
  <a data-text-id="14313043397573033985" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_481985205" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/481985205" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/481985205?book_show_action=true">Dec 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-standalone">series-standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer481985205" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3538979552927391939"><b>LOVE THIS BOOK! SERIOUSLY, LOVE IT!</b><br/><br/>Maysie is a junior at College. She is 20 years old, lives with her best friend, Riley, is in a sorority which she loves, and is sort-of dating a slacker stoner who doesn’t really do a lot for her, but she is happy to go along with it for now. Most importantly, she is doing what she wants, and enjoying life away from the constant disapproval of her parents. She does seem a bit selfish and immature at times, but I kept reminding myself that she is only 20. I was </span>
  <span id="freeText3538979552927391939" style="display:none"><b>LOVE THIS BOOK! SERIOUSLY, LOVE IT!</b><br><br>Maysie is a junior at College. She is 20 years old, lives with her best friend, Riley, is in a sorority which she loves, and is sort-of dating a slacker stoner who doesn’t really do a lot for her, but she is happy to go along with it for now. Most importantly, she is doing what she wants, and enjoying life away from the constant disapproval of her parents. She does seem a bit selfish and immature at times, but I kept reminding myself that she is only 20. I was completely clueless when I was 20 so I’m not about to judge!<br><br>Maysie’s carefree lifestyle comes to a grinding halt when she receives a massive bill in the mail, and she discovers she’s been a little bit too carefree with her parent’s credit card. With her parents demanding she pay them back, Maysie applies for a job at a local bar, and it is there that she meets gorgeous, hot bartender, Jordan Levitt.<br><br>OMGOMGOMG! Excuse me while I go all fangirl for a moment, because Jordan is absolutely AMAZING!!! <i>“He was gorgeous, he played in a band, he was a freaking frat boy and he had the whole tattoo, piercing thing going on.”</i> Oh, and he rides a motorbike and has a heart of gold! Squeeeeeeeeee!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383382853i/6530227._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jordan makes it very clear that he’s attracted to her from the very beginning, with lots of smiles, winks, passing touches and meaningful glances. The chemistry between them is glaringly obvious, and then comes the news that Jordan has a girlfriend. Whaaat? Yep! And not just any girlfriend, she is the President of Maysie’s sorority, and the two of them are the campus golden couple. <br><br>Broken hearted and still hopelessly attracted to him, Maysie does her best to keep her distance from Jordan, who doesn’t give up his pursuit of her. Which leads me to my one big question – why did he not just break up with his girlfriend? Seriously? I don’t know. Especially when he’s spouting off lines like this…<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Maysie, I have a girlfriend. A girlfriend I’ve been with for three goddamn years.”<br>… Jordan opened his eyes and looked at me as he grabbed my face between his hands and held me perfectly still, not letting me move. “But tell me, Mays, why is it that all I can fucking think about is you? Why am I so eager to take another guy’s head off for touching you? Why is it when I lay in bed at night I wish it was you there beside me?”</i>
</blockquote><br>Whoa *fans self*. Intense, huh! The whole thing had a very <i>Thoughtless</i> feel to it. The nasty love triangle, the heartbreaking angst, and the whole vibe just felt very similar. But this book takes a drastic turn in direction when Maysie and Jordan hook up one night, and are discovered. Rumours start to fly around campus, and Maysie is turned into a pariah overnight. Trying her best to move on, Jordan ditches his girlfriend, and the two of them finally come together in an intense, passionate, all-encompassing romance. And It. Is. Awesome!!! <br><br><blockquote>“<i>This is more than just physical attraction and you know it. I have NEVER wanted someone the way I want you. This thing I feel for you isn't rational. It doesn't really make sense, but it's there. And I'll be damned if I let you run away from it just because you feel insecure. Because there is no other girl for me, Mays. You are it.”</i>
</blockquote><br>I absolutely adore these two together! Every little moment was gorgeous – the banter, the laughs, the tender moments, and the scorching hotness. Phew! And even when Maysie is struggling with her bad reputation that continues to spread around campus, Jordan is there to pull her out of it. He’s so freaking functional, and is so in love with Maysie that he’s prepared to do anything to make it work, and I love him for it. Seriously, the man is made of awesome. <br><br>But with the rocky foundation to their relationship, jealousies, and Maysie’s continually spiralling reputation thanks to horrendous bullying by bitchy girls out to make her life miserable, these two have a lot against them, and it makes for one very tough, emotional, and angst-filled ride. And the emotion! OMG, the emotion! I was devastated at all that they go through, and watching Jordan pour his heart out was heartbreaking!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I thought you were worth everything. That we were worth all the drama and bullshit. I am willing to fight to the death for what we have. But I can only do that if you're willing to fight with me.”</i>
</blockquote><br>But I loved it, I utterly, utterly loved it! Yes, some of Maysie’s actions are questionable (and downright stupid), and she falls apart a lot, but she’s young, she’s still discovering who she is, and I found that I could really empathise with her. <br><br>There is a fantastic supporting cast – Maysie’s girlfriends, and Jordan’s bandmates are all spectators to the unfolding drama, and I can’t wait for future books in the series as we get to see their stories. <br><br>I am declaring myself a mad fan of A. Meredith Walters, I love the way she writes! I wasn’t originally sure that I’d like this book, but she sucked me right in from the very start, and I couldn’t put it down. Even with all of the heartache, I was completely swept away by Maysie and Jordan’s story, I did think the ending was a little bit abrupt <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I wanted Maysie's declaration to be bigger and more meaningful than what it was - especially after everything that she had put him through <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but I was left grinning like an idiot and flying high from all of the swoon.<br><br>4.5 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3538979552927391939" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_472970771" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/472970771" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/472970771?book_show_action=true">Dec 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula " href="/user/show/2879703-paula">Paula </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer472970771" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10511869082230315834"><br/><i>
  <b>"Who gives a damn about their reputation? Oh, that would be me! Especially since mine had gone straight to hell in the span of thirty minutes"</b>
</i><br/><br/>Sorority girl Maysie Ardin has made some bad choices lately. She's not doing so well in school, she's dating a loser and, instead of using the credit card her parents gave her for emergency use only, she bought expensive clothing. And now she has racked up a $3500 bill. Her parents are not happy. It's time for Maysie to get her priorities straight. Fir</span>
  <span id="freeText10511869082230315834" style="display:none"><br /><i>
  <b>"Who gives a damn about their reputation? Oh, that would be me! Especially since mine had gone straight to hell in the span of thirty minutes"</b>
</i><br /><br />Sorority girl Maysie Ardin has made some bad choices lately. She's not doing so well in school, she's dating a loser and, instead of using the credit card her parents gave her for emergency use only, she bought expensive clothing. And now she has racked up a $3500 bill. Her parents are not happy. It's time for Maysie to get her priorities straight. First thing she needs to do, get a second job to pay off her credit card.<br /><br />When Maysie goes to apply for a serving job with her best friend, Riley, they are both immediately hired on the spot. She also meets the sexy, tattooed, pierced, rock star Jordan Levitt, who she has instant chemistry with. But things aren't always as they seem. And when Maysie finds out Jordan has a girlfriend, and who his girlfriend is, she does her best to stay away from him no matter how much she is drawn to him. No matter how much she thinks about him. No matter what...he is off-limits.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“I wanted to tell you that I couldn't stop thinking about your face. That you had burrowed your way so deep into my veins that I would fucking bleed you. That if I died tomorrow, I could go a happy man for having felt your lips on my skin.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Jordan Levitt is the popular, gorgeous, rocker who all the girls want a piece of. He is also the president of his fraternity. His relationship with his girlfriend has simmered down. So when he meets Maysie, she is someone that he has a lot in common with. She is more interested in him, and his music, than his own girlfriend. This kind of chemistry he has with Maysie is new to him, something he's never felt before. And because of that fierce chemistry they have together, he is willing to betray his trust with his girlfriend to be with Maysie, and relentlessly pursue her until she finally gives in to him.<br /><br />Maysie does her best to stay away from Jordan. She knew the consequences would be bad if anything happen with Jordan. But unfortunately she could no longer deny her attraction to Jordan. And because of <i>one kiss</i>, her whole reputation was ruined. <br /><br />Jordan Levitt is the popular, gorgeous, rocker who all the girls want a piece of. He is also the president of his fraternity. His relationship with his girlfriend has simmered down. So when he meets Maysie, she is someone that he has a lot in common with. She is more interested in him, and his music, than his own girlfriend. The kind of chemistry he has with Maysie is new to him, something he's never felt before. And because of that fierce chemistry they have together, he is willing to betray his trust with his girlfriend to be with Maysie, and relentlessly pursue her until she finally gives in to him.<br /><br />Maysie does her best to stay away from Jordan. She knew the consequences would be bad if anything happened with him. But, unfortunately, she could no longer deny her attraction to Jordan. And because of one kiss, her whole reputation was ruined.<br /><br />Because of this kiss, Maysie endures a lot of vicious rumors and cattiness. And, because of that one kiss, the life she has created for herself is completely shredded overnight. It's really hard to stomach the things that are said about her. Her sorority sisters are the epitome of mean girls. They are shallow and very immature. The guys weren't any better. To say they put her through hell is a massive understatement. Yet Maysie refused to quit the sorority. Instead, she hopes things get better and the girls will accept her again. Which was ridiculously stupid if you ask me. Those horrible girls were not her friends.<br /><br />I did understand Maysie's insecurities about wanting to fit in. She was the wallflower in high school. And in college, she wanted to feel popular and important for the first time in her life. A lot of her insecurities stem from the way her father treats her, as if she was never good enough to be his daughter. But is it really worth being friends with girls who mistreat you so badly just to be popular, to be a part of a group? To feel accepted? No, it's not worth it and Maysie learns this lesson the hard way.<br /><br />I had some serious anxiety and frustration while reading this story. This is a common story, where the woman is to blame and called a whore because she is the “other” woman. I've never understood why the woman always takes the blame. It takes two people to cheat! Also, it really aggravated me when Maysie always ran from her problems. She never stood up for herself. Maysie's logic drove me bat-shit crazy! She does have some character growth by the end of the story. It's definitely a great moment to see her FINALLY get the last word.<br /><br />This story is about love, trust, and acceptance. Sometimes love isn't enough to build a relationship. There must be trust. Both Jordan and Maysie have some severe trust issues especially because of the way the relationship started. Can two people who have committed the ultimate betrayal learn to trust one another? And the true issue that lies within this story is acceptance. Maysie needs to learn to accept herself. To be herself. To find herself. And to stop caring about what other people think of her.<br /><br />Overall, I liked this book. It held my interest and I read it in almost one sitting. Fair warning, though, Maysie will frustrate the hell out of you. <br /><br />Rating: C+<br />Heat: HOT<br /><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Find us on <a href="https://twitter.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://facebook.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> too!</i>
</b></span>

  <span id="freeText15755399583263270073" style="display:none">What do you get when you mix all the following?<br /><br />A $3,500 credit card bill for a pair of Manolo Blahnik sandals and a “Vitamin A” bikini screams the demand for a second job for college junior Maysie Aldin.<br /><br />A roommate and best friend with some common sense, who offers up a solution to Maysie’s money problems and many many more as time goes by.<br /><br />A waitressing job at the local college hangout, Barton’s Pub.<br /><br />A flirty and sexy bartender named, Jordan Levitt, who is a mixture of tatted-up bad boy and gorgeous boy-next-door who at first sight sets your panties on fire. <br /><br />A sorority house full of self-absorbed, hateful, and mean “sisters” that takes the word cruel to new heights, along with a fraternity house that overflows with horny guys who are just as self-absorbed and mean.<br /> <br />And, oh yeah, the big OH NO!!! That bartender Maysie has fallen head over heels for – well he’s been in a serious relationship for three years and it’s still ongoing. With the way he's pursuing Maysie, one wonders if he has forgotten all about his girlfriend. Her name is Olivia and she’s one of Maysie’s sorority sisters and is also the President of said sorority! <br /><br />And you’ll have to read the book to get the rest of the story. One thing is for sure: All mixed together, you're certain to receive a captivating and riveting roller coaster ride which equals a grand old afternoon of reading! Highly recommend. <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_490851565" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/490851565" />
    <a title="Fiction And Fashion Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14899217-fiction-and-fashion-book-blog"><img alt="Fiction And Fashion Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1355331911p2/14899217.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/490851565?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fiction And Fashion Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fiction And Fashion Book Blog" href="/user/show/14899217-fiction-and-fashion-book-blog">Fiction And Fashion Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer490851565" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12012367609535903942">Ultimately 3.5 Stars...But definitely a 4 Star at times!<br/><br/><b>"At what point did parties go from 'hey lets hang out' to 'I'm gonna drink shots from between your boobs?'"</b><br/><br/>I really didn't know what to expect when I bought Bad Rep, but boy was I pleasantly surprised! The character's were awesome, the dialog was entertaining, and the romance was hot! I absolutely love books that take place in college. It's like reliving my keg stand glory days (not like I still do keg stands anymore or anything...), but si</span>
  <span id="freeText12012367609535903942" style="display:none">Ultimately 3.5 Stars...But definitely a 4 Star at times!<br /><br /><b>"At what point did parties go from 'hey lets hang out' to 'I'm gonna drink shots from between your boobs?'"</b><br /><br />I really didn't know what to expect when I bought Bad Rep, but boy was I pleasantly surprised! The character's were awesome, the dialog was entertaining, and the romance was hot! I absolutely love books that take place in college. It's like reliving my keg stand glory days (not like I still do keg stands anymore or anything...), but since this college romance also gave me a peek into the not so glamorous lives of sororities and fraternities it made it even more delicious and impossible to put down!<br /><br /><b>"I love being in Chi Delta, but there's more to life than cupcakes and talking to random people about how much I love sparkles."</b><br /><br />This book was FILLED with drama! Not the gut wrenching, life altering drama that has been filling my kindle up lately, but the kind of petty drama that makes you roll your eyes a bit. You know, the gossipy, back stabbing, girl fight drama that is entertaining to read, but gets old after a while. Fortunately, Jordan and Maysie's journey to love and trust far out shines all the annoying bickering. Their attraction was immediate (and understandable) and like I said before, their romance was insanely hot!<br /><br /><b>"Dear Lord, the flash of his white teeth was like a hot button to my nether regions. Down vagina! Down girl."</b><br /><br /><b>"Holy bad boy Batman!"</b> Jordan Levitt was AMAZING and completely owned this book! If guys like Jordan are what is hanging out at those smelly Frat houses, then sign me the hell up! Luckily for me, Jordan is not the typical frat boy, he's just your run of the mill tattooed and pierced, rock star drummer who happens to be the President of his fraternity. Sounds like the guys I went to college with....riiighhhttt! You will absolutely LOVE Jordan, this guy is jaw dropping (as well as panty dropping...). There is a reason he was giving the nickname of the "Piper" ;) All joking aside, this guy totally stole my heart and is my new favorite Bad Boy Book Boyfriend!<br /><br /><b>But tell me, Mays, why is it that all I can fucking think about it you? Why am I so eager to take another guy's head off for touching you? Why is it when I lay in bed at night I wish it was you there beside me?"</b><br /><br />Maysie, Oh Mays... How I want to shake that pretty little brunette head of yours. I get it, the girls got her issues, we here at Fiction and Fashion can probably relate better than anyone to a girl with an expensive shoe habit, but the whining and insecurities were just too much! She was so lucky to have a friend like Riley to balance out the crazy. Actually all of Maysie's friends (Vivian, Gracie and even Eli) helped me get over the fact that I sort of wanted her to choke on one of those nasty cigarettes she was always smoking. Even though she was not my favorite character, I did recognize the intense weight that Maysie had on her shoulders and get that guilt can make you do crazy things. I also did truly believe Maysie's love for Jordan and her "sisters" and felt bad for her... Then I remembered she had Jordan Levitt in her bed every night and my sympathy went right out the window!<br /><br /><b>"Why couldn't I get over my insecurities? Oh, That's right. Because I was a neurotic, self-sabotager extraordinaire. Hell, if ruining something great were an olympic sport, I would have the gold medal."</b><br /><br />I honestly wasn't expecting this book to be so freaking funny. Riley was absolutely hilarious and I LOVED all the pop culture references. I cannot think of a better way to put your life into perspective than by comparing it to characters from 90210. For the record though, I was ALWAYS team Kelly..Brenda's a bitch!<br /><br /><b>"I've always thought you were better than those stupid Chi Smelltas or whatever the fuck they're called."</b><br /><br />I would recommend this book to anyone looking for a fun and sexy read. It's probably not a story you will take a ton away from and remember for the rest of your life, but I'm pretty sure you'll take away some sweet Jordan memories :)<br /><br />Reviewed by Abby for <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.FictionandFashion.com">www.FictionandFashion.com</a><br /></span>

<div id="review_457700621" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/457700621" />
    <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11270628-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1355970351p2/11270628.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/457700621?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/11270628-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer457700621" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4610255583840411480">****$ .99 on Amazon! 12/26****<br/>_________________________<br/><br/><b>Is self-worth really found in the opinions of others?</b><br/><br/>Twenty-year-old Maysie Ardin finally has independence from her very conservative parents. She’s about to start her junior year of college and is a proud member of Chi Delta sorority. A shopping spree with her sorority sisters lands her $3,500 in debt…with her parent’s credit card. In order to pay off her debt, Maysie is forced to take on a second job. She finds a waitressing job at a local</span>
  <span id="freeText4610255583840411480" style="display:none">****$ .99 on Amazon! 12/26****<br />_________________________<br /><br /><b>Is self-worth really found in the opinions of others?</b><br /><br />Twenty-year-old Maysie Ardin finally has independence from her very conservative parents. She’s about to start her junior year of college and is a proud member of Chi Delta sorority. A shopping spree with her sorority sisters lands her $3,500 in debt…with her parent’s credit card. In order to pay off her debt, Maysie is forced to take on a second job. She finds a waitressing job at a local bar. That’s where she meets Jordan Livett. <br /><br /><i>“You have taken my heart, every inch of me, Maysie. I don’t know that I have anything else to give you that you don’t already have.” <br />–Jordan</i><br /><br />OH. MY. GOD. Jordan Levitt, is dreamy. He’s a hot frat boy tattooed bartender with multiple piercings who moonlights as a drummer. Oh, and he sings. He’s instantly attracted to Maysie. So what’s the problem? He has a girlfriend, Olivia. Olivia is the president of Maysie’s sorority. Jordan is a senior and attending the same college as Maysie. Avoiding Jordan is impossible. She finally gives into her desires and gets caught by one of her “sisters”. Oops! Now labeled the college whore, Maysie must learn to deal with her new role at school. <br /><br /><i>“I wish I could stop feeling like Kelly Taylor splitting up Dylan and Brenda.” <br />–Maysie</i><br /><br />Gossip, catfights, backstabbing, cheating, sisterhood, friendship, jealousy, sex, and love all tested as Maysie learns how to look beyond what others think. We watch her grow up and face the music. She’s always based her life on what others think, but when it slaps her in the face (literally) she must learn love and respect herself first before she can expect it from others. <br /><br /><i>“Why does the opinion of every other jackass on campus matter more than how you and I feel?”<br />-Jordan</i><br /><br />Bad Rep was a great story about love and acceptance. Maysie and Jordan’s journey was rocky and insanely <b>HOT</b>! This is one of those books you won’t be able to put down. You never know what is going to happen next. Reading this made me glad I wasn’t 20 anymore. I do not miss all the drama, but I love to read about it. The author wrote Maysie as a very real and believable person. You will connect with her and feel every emotion. You will laugh with her, cry with her, and yell at her. Do not miss out on this book! It is a must read for anyone who likes drama and dreamy boys. You won’t be able to put it down!!<br /><br /><i>“And I don’t give a fuck if you like me. Or if the Chi Delts think I’m the biggest whore this side of the Appalachian Mountains. I am done worrying about what everyone thinks about me. Because all that counts is that I like me. So the rest of you can go to hell.” <br />–Maysie</i><br /><br /><b>P.S.</b><br />I thought I should mention this. I caught this in the Acknowledgments. The author was thanking some of her special people, <i>“Particularly my wonderful husband, who is the true inspiration for Jordan and all his kick ass, rock god ways. We met in a bar. He was the sexy, guitar playing Brit and I couldn’t resist. &lt;3 Thank you for just being you.”</i> <b>Ummmm….OMG!</b> Just knowing that Jordan was based on a real person made the story that much better. You are a lucky lady! Please feel free to post a picture ;-)</span>
  <a data-text-id="4610255583840411480" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_442780424" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/442780424" />
    <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite"><img alt="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368215503p2/3758447.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/442780424?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=so-disappointed">so-disappointed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=made-me-roll-my-eyes">made-me-roll-my-eyes</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer442780424" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3200382442909773555">I'm afraid this is shaping up to be the year of "everyone liked it but me" and it sucks. <br/><br/>I wanted to love this book. I adored the other book I read by this author - Find you in the Dark so I was really looking forward to this one. <br/><br/>I liked the last 7%, but that wasn't enough to make up for all that came before for me. <br/><br/>I'm always a harsh judge of cheating in a plot line - so I know that was part of my problem. I had a hard time liking Jordan after the crap he pulled in the beginning. I just still </span>
  <span id="freeText3200382442909773555" style="display:none">I'm afraid this is shaping up to be the year of "everyone liked it but me" and it sucks. <br /><br />I wanted to love this book. I adored the other book I read by this author - Find you in the Dark so I was really looking forward to this one. <br /><br />I liked the last 7%, but that wasn't enough to make up for all that came before for me. <br /><br />I'm always a harsh judge of cheating in a plot line - so I know that was part of my problem. I had a hard time liking Jordan after the crap he pulled in the beginning. I just still can't understand why he didn't break up with Olivia when he decided to pursue Mays. Also, I could never get over his whole " I don't knew why the fact I have a girlfriend is a deal breaker" attitude. He comes off as this stand up guy in the end, but that never jived for me with who he was in the beginning. It just made all those swoon-worthy lines fall totally flat for me. <br /><br />And Maysie drove me nuts - but not in a good way. I get that the thrust of the book was to show her growth from someone who cared to much about what everyone thought to someone who thought for herself - and that was nice to see (and was why I liked the last 7%) but her overwhelming insecurity and ability to self destruct make her a very unappealing character for me for most of the book. Even in light of the horrible bullying, I didn't like her enough to care too much. <br /><br />The last issue I had was that I felt like the reaction of the other people on campus to the whole cheating thing was beyond unrealistic. I have seen similar situations play out in real life, both in a college setting, and beyond, but never has the public condemnation come close to that level. Hell, most people (outside of the actual parties involved) barely batted an eye. It certainly wouldn't have taken weeks to blow over. <br /><br />Anyway -this has gotten great reviews from most of my good reads friends - so I hope I don't put anyone off reading this. I still love this author - and I'm waiting with baited breath for the follow up to Find You in the Dark. This one just wasn't for me. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3200382442909773555" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/472961399" />
    <a title="Mitchii" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4808951-mitchii"><img alt="Mitchii" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605348765p2/4808951.jpg" /></a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808951-mitchii?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808951-mitchii?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808951-mitchii?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808951-mitchii?shelf=self-published">self-published</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808951-mitchii?shelf=realistic-fiction">realistic-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808951-mitchii?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer472961399" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15176810846417186860">So here’s the gist. She splurged and needs the money to pay back so she decided to find a job. She found a job…and a guy. She and the guy has this undeniable attraction, she didn’t mind the flirting. She thought it was harmless or so she thought because luck runs out when she found out he has girlfriend and she’s the president of the sorority she belong to. Damn luck, right?<br/><br/>But the worst has yet to come, although they tried (they weren’t really trying hard to ignore their attraction) they eventu</span>
  <span id="freeText15176810846417186860" style="display:none">So here’s the gist. She splurged and needs the money to pay back so she decided to find a job. She found a job…and a guy. She and the guy has this undeniable attraction, she didn’t mind the flirting. She thought it was harmless or so she thought because luck runs out when she found out he has girlfriend and she’s the president of the sorority she belong to. Damn luck, right?<br /><br />But the worst has yet to come, although they tried (they weren’t really trying hard to ignore their attraction) they eventually caved in they make out and was busted by his girlfriend’s friend and also member of her sorority. News went out and people has labeled he names, like slut, whore for making a move with the guy that supposed to be off limits. Is her reputation beyond salvation? Is he worth the trash talking she’s getting from everyone?<br /><br />Those questions what kept me reading this book, and it did have that answers to that but it was hard connecting with the philosophy when the characters annoyed you to death. I didn’t like how self-centered she was…most of the time. The only time I commend her was when she stand up for herself (which was freaking about time because name calling has got to stop!). Even the guy needs to stand up for her girlfriend, he’s aware of the backlash she’ll get once they are out in public but he wasn’t there for her. Not really. He only did was to console privately and that’s not enough no matter how much he assured her that she’s it for him.<br /><br />This is one problem when relationship started in cheating. The trust. No matter how much the ex had treated him, she still deserves to know that you’ll end the relationship. You need to cut the ties first before you hop to another prospect. No wonder she was jealous and paranoid, because they betrayed someone. But her jealousy is all too consuming that I have to prevent myself from pulling my hair because I spend a fortune on it. But to cut my whining short, they did make their relationship works. They find out the true villain. They’re now in talking terms with his ex. It looked happily ever after to me. I’m just here wondering why I’m not satisfied.<br /><br />It wasn’t a bad read but I was having a hard time keeping up with the characters annoying decisions and actions. This book mostly centered on their relationship, a relationship under people’s radar. Some family issues as to why the girl was reluctant at first to try real relationship, and the guy pursing the career he had chosen for himself. But they, as I said, overcome it. Another all’s well that ends well tale, I guess. </span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer477797574" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer827898673028300383">4.5 Stars!<br/><br/>Check out more reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com'>http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br/><br/>I absolutely adored the characters in this book. The author did a wonderful, fantastic job in the character development of this book. She was so descriptive and punched me in the face with the character connection I felt.<br/><br/><br/><br/>Maysie is a dynamic character. We are put through so much with her. My favorite thing aobut her was her confidence and seeing that confidence crumble--crushed me. She is such a relatable character. Ever</span>
  <span id="freeText827898673028300383" style="display:none">4.5 Stars!<br /><br />Check out more reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br /><br />I absolutely adored the characters in this book. The author did a wonderful, fantastic job in the character development of this book. She was so descriptive and punched me in the face with the character connection I felt.<br /><br /><br /><br />Maysie is a dynamic character. We are put through so much with her. My favorite thing aobut her was her confidence and seeing that confidence crumble--crushed me. She is such a relatable character. Every way she turned, I saw myself. <br /><br /><br /><br />I loved feeling that instant attraction between Jordan and Maysie.<br /><br /><br /><br />"Down Vagina! Down Girl."<br /><br /><br /><br />Their pull was so strong and it continued to suck me in!<br /><br /><br /><br />"Holy bad boy Batman!"<br /><br /><br /><br />Jordan.....Jordan......Jordan.....<br /><br />I loved him---I hated him---I loved him again. He put me through the ringer. I kept picturing him in my mind and I don't think I could do him justice. I think he is off the charts when it comes to bad ass hotness. As I was reading, I could hear him beat on the drums and sing directly to me...yummy!<br /><br /><br /><br />The chemistry between Jordan &amp; Maysie was electrifying! The build up of their relationship was intense. The bedroom (well some were in the bedroom) scenes were smoking, realistic and very HOT!<br /><br /><br /><br />"Damn had he seriously just screwed my brains out behind a dilapidated old shed in the middle of a party? Yes, he had."<br /><br /><br /><br />I also loved the college/sorority/fraternity storyline. It was so realistic and dead on! It took me back to a time and place where I was young and carefree! :)<br /><br /><br /><br />I can't finish this review without talking about the secondary characters. Riley, Olivia, Milla, Gracie, Viv and Eli. Even though they were in the background the author did a wonderful job at connecting them to me as the reader. I loved some (Riley); hated some (Milla); annoyed by some (Olivia, Eli); made friends with some (Gracie and Viv), but each held a very special place in the storyline. <br /><br /><br /><br />Overall, wonderful read! Highly recommend to all who like college romance!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="827898673028300383" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4825603-amanda"><img alt="Amanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1309958279p2/4825603.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/488223762?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/4825603-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4825603-amanda?shelf=2012">2012</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer488223762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14277586212748169193">Here's the thing, this could have been an absolutely amazing book. It could have, had the main character been nothing like what was written. <br/><br/>Maysie was an absolute terrible character. She was whiny, insecure, stubborn, and just a really terrible character. Anytime anything went wrong, she ran and hid. Seriously, she freaking hid under her blankets. <br/><br/>Now, don't get me wrong, sometimes life sucks and you get some shitty stuff thrown your way. Especially if you make the decision to follow through on</span>
  <span id="freeText14277586212748169193" style="display:none">Here's the thing, this could have been an absolutely amazing book. It could have, had the main character been nothing like what was written. <br /><br />Maysie was an absolute terrible character. She was whiny, insecure, stubborn, and just a really terrible character. Anytime anything went wrong, she ran and hid. Seriously, she freaking hid under her blankets. <br /><br />Now, don't get me wrong, sometimes life sucks and you get some shitty stuff thrown your way. Especially if you make the decision to follow through on some hot lustful attraction with a very popular guy who is dating a very popular girl. SHIT IS GOING TO FLY YOUR WAY. I didn't know whether to laugh, shake my head, or throw my hands up when she acted surprised when the entire sorority house turned on her after she was caught. I mean really? What normal girl would think everything would smell like roses and that she would be excepted by the girls that were under the leadership of the scorned girl. OMG, this chick was mental. <br /><br />Then you have the boy. I'll admit that I actually adored him. Even though he was a bit mixed up and made some bad decisions, you could tell he was kind of a level headed sweet guy. So, you won't be surprised when I found myself rooting for him to go find another girl and leave Maysie's ass behind. Ugh, she annoyed the snot out of me. <br /><br />The best part (and by that, I mean worst part) of this whole book was that most of her trouble with Jordan was self manufactured in her head because she refused to communicate with him. Honestly, if I could get my money back for this book, I totally would. <br /><br />So, your probably wondering why the 2 star review rather than the 1 star review. I will tell you, I actually enjoyed the story if I focused on the surrounding characters (Grace, Vivian, the band, Eli, Riley, Damien, etc). I actually enjoyed them and Riley made me laugh. I don't feel like the book was a horrible waste because some of the characters were great. It really was just Maysie that ruined this whole book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14277586212748169193" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_449676689" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449676689" />
    <a title="Megan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2090085-megan"><img alt="Megan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574714802p2/2090085.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/449676689?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Megan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Megan" href="/user/show/2090085-megan">Megan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=novels">novels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=coming-of-age">coming-of-age</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=music">music</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=2012-2">2012-2</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=relationships">relationships</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=school">school</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2090085-megan?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>,

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449676689" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13072288196984364375">"Bad Rep" by A. Meredith Walters 4.5/5 Stars<br/><br/>“Dear lord, the flash of his gleaming white teeth was like a hot button to my nether regions. Down vagina! Down, girl.”<br/><br/>There are plenty of laugh-out-loud moments in 'Bad Rep', but those are not the only reason to fall in love with the story (and Jordan).<br/><br/>The story is told from the point of view of Maysie, a twenty year old college junior who falls head-over-heels for her sexy, off-limits coworker Jordan. Jordan also falls for Maysie, and their relations</span>
  <span id="freeText13072288196984364375" style="display:none">"Bad Rep" by A. Meredith Walters 4.5/5 Stars<br /><br />“Dear lord, the flash of his gleaming white teeth was like a hot button to my nether regions. Down vagina! Down, girl.”<br /><br />There are plenty of laugh-out-loud moments in 'Bad Rep', but those are not the only reason to fall in love with the story (and Jordan).<br /><br />The story is told from the point of view of Maysie, a twenty year old college junior who falls head-over-heels for her sexy, off-limits coworker Jordan. Jordan also falls for Maysie, and their relationship is hot but messy. Maysie and Jordan must navigate the consequences of their relationship and each others insecurities to attempt to make their relationship work. <br /><br />Maysie is far from perfect—one of the reader's first glimpses of here is as she explains her reason for using her emergency credit card and thus needing a second job, “Not even I could explain how I justified my Manolo Blahnik heeled sandals as an emergency. But damn, they had looked amazing with my fitted red sundress.” As the story progresses, the reader discovers she also has poor self-esteem, major parental issues, and difficulty facing her problems.<br /><br />Despite Maysie's flaws, I was quite proud of her for keeping her promise to herself of not being the 'other woman' for as long as she did. I'm not sure how she resisted a guy who she describes as having a deep voice that “you imagine hearing in a bedroom. After naughty sex. The kind of voice that was a combination of the most decadent chocolate and outright sin.” Her other initial response to Jordan was to think to herself, “Okay, Jordan was hot. Like ridiculously hot. He had a delicious edge about him that was hard to ignore. He was this weird mixture of tatted up bad boy and gorgeous guy next door.”<br /><br />If you are not intrigued by Jordan by now, my friends, you must not be paying attention.<br /><br />Ok, so we've established so far that Jordan is hot, and Maysie, like any normal human being, is not immune to him. That being said, the characters are well-developed and three dimensional. While reading, it's not difficult to become entrenched in their trials and triumphs. I went through many phases of both loving and hating Maysie and Jordan. I cheered for them, cried for them, and yelled at them. One does not yell things like “get over your daddy issues already!” at a fictional character unless she has become invested in the happiness of said character. <br /><br />Not only did Ms. Walters do a fantastic job in creating emotion, she also did a great job in creating atmosphere. While Maysie was at Barton's, I felt I was right there alongside her working in a restaurant. From the way the employees interact with one another to the smells of grease and the tasks the employees perform, the experience of reading about working as a waitress is very real. (I can say that with authority, having worked as a waitress many times!)<br /><br />This story is definitely a win for new adult fiction! I can't resist reading about tatted-up, bad boys, and this story definitely provided that for me in abundance. Let me reiterate: Jordan is one of the the sweetest and hottest bad boys to ever grace fiction with his presence. I can't wait to re-read 'Bad Rep' when it's released officially on December 21!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13072288196984364375" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer444999336" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17532339080732533737">This book had me up until 5am. I couldn't put it down without knowing how it ended. The first 40% I was wanting to pull out my hair. Guy has girlfriend, likes other girl. Flirting back and forth. I though, oh great, another love triangle with an indecisive person. But the thing is, Jordan was never at odds with what he felt for Maysie. The connection was instant for him and Maysie too. She just fought it harder. She was very emotional when it came to what others thought of her, and it makes sens</span>
  <span id="freeText17532339080732533737" style="display:none">This book had me up until 5am. I couldn't put it down without knowing how it ended. The first 40% I was wanting to pull out my hair. Guy has girlfriend, likes other girl. Flirting back and forth. I though, oh great, another love triangle with an indecisive person. But the thing is, Jordan was never at odds with what he felt for Maysie. The connection was instant for him and Maysie too. She just fought it harder. She was very emotional when it came to what others thought of her, and it makes sense coming from how she was raised. Never good enough. Was it a D-bag move to ask her out while having a girlfriend? yep. But Jordan was really anything but a D- bag. I loved him! He was sweet, thoughtful, attentive and romantic. Poor Maysie just couldn't get past her crap to see how great they really were together. So She had to suffer, which in turn made him suffer which made me suffer!! I wanted to bitch slap her! This book was great, held me captive until the last page. They both learned valuable lessons that worked in the end. Plus, some great sexy steamy scenes!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17532339080732533737" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText10106750140959105788" style="display:none">I recommend this to every freaking body!<br /><br />AHHHHHHHHHHHHH! So SIKED to have read this. So BUMMED that it had to end. Next to SEXY in the dictionary is a picture of a lean, short dark haired, pierced and tatted hottie named Jordan. I promise you you will come all over yourself at just the mention of his name after reading this. Holy fuck! <br /><br />I'm salivating. Sorry.<br /><br />The drama! //<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('W0O7UtYy70IC+W/s6wgBDrgFfeT4i5/CVVEBhEo53YyAGZUUTy21WUCpvx3nNcOWE6xPJtJWCJipSB9nwKQExw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yW3vVZpdUGoQws6IeF7wSuv2COFIRjSK3aFkVAnFRtESN8ETA0IKcVKSHnl0YzLSQF86I2Kbo9AhuHq3g1ifmg==')})
  }
//]]>

When Rowan finds herself at Logan’s mercy after he inadvertently learns of the abuse she has suffered at the hands of her father, their lives become intertwined in a way neither ever imagined nor wanted.\n\nIn an effort to protect her, but with his own hands tied by her unwillingness to report the abuse, Logan strikes a deal requiring Rowan to stay with him whenever there is a chance her father might be on a drunken binge—which is often.
